<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зодчий.html>зо́дчий</a> (27724)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зьдъчии</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zĭdŭčii</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">potter, builder, bricklayer, mason</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зьдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zĭdŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stone wall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зьдати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zĭdati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zьdati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to build</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***золотивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:золотивший.html>золоти́вший</a> (29931)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотивший.html>золоти́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zolotívšij</span>)

***золото.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лото</a> (2223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лото</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoloto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zolto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰolh₃tom</i> (o-grade), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰelh₃-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">yellow; gleam; to shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злато.html>зла́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zláto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">złoto</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">зла̑то</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">zelts</i> (e-grade), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gold</i> (zero grade)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золото́й</a> (8547)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лото</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zóloto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золото́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zolotój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gold; golden
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золота́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:монета.html>моне́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zolotája</b> monéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>gold</b> coin</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>gold, golden <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dear, precious</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золото́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zolotój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золото́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золоты́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золоты́х</a></b>)

<p>Back-formation from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зонтик.html>зо́нтик</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zóntik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зонт.html>зонт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zont</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зонт.html>зонта́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зонт.html>зонты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зонт.html>зонто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>umbrella</li>
<li>sunshade, parasol</li>
<li>canopy, awning</li>
<li>cupola</li>
<li>hood (of furnace)</li></ol>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зр(еть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zr(etʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зоркий.html>зо́ркий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zórkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зо́рче</b>)

***зоркость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зоркость.html>зо́ркость</a> (29018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зоркий.html>зо́ркий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zórkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зоркость.html>зо́ркость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zórkostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зоркость.html>зо́ркости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зоркость.html>зо́ркости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зоркость.html>зо́ркостей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vigilance, watchfulness</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zrělъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зрелый.html>зре́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zrélyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зреле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зреле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mature</li>
<li>ripe</li></ol>

***зреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зреть</a> (15023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zьrěti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to ripen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зреть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zretʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:созреть.html>созре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ripen, to mature
<dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><b><i>c.</i> 1920</b>, Сергей Буданцев, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:мятеж.html>Мяте́ж</a></i> <br /><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голове́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:командующий.html>кома́ндующего</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зре́ют</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:благой.html>благи́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a>:<dl><dd>good thoughts <b>are ripening</b> in the commander's head</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><b>1897</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>К</a>. Гермониус, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ясный.html>Я́сной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поляна.html>Поля́не</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Льва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстого</a></i> <br /><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тень.html>тени</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудный.html>чу́дные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:липа.html>ли́п</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> берез <a href = vnd.unilang:создаваться.html>создава́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зре́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудный.html>чу́дные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образ.html>о́бразы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:художественный.html>худо́жественные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́ны</a>:<dl><dd>here in the shadow of lovely lindens and birches wondrous images and artistic paintings were created and <b>ripened</b></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зьрѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zĭrěti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zьrěti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see, to look at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">žiūrėti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зреть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zretʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узреть.html>узре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to watch, to look at</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зря.html>зря</a> (1431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зря.html>зря</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zrja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in vain, to no avail, for nothing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зря.html>Зря</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zrja ty éto skazál. Tepérʹ vesʹ górod búdet znatʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You shouldn't have said that. Now the whole town will know.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зря.html>Зря</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́лись</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:равно.html>равно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оценить.html>оцени́л</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zrja my starálisʹ. Vsjó ravnó niktó ne oceníl.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">All our efforts were in vain. Nobody appreciated them.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
